Made it far more difficult to pass than I think any other driver would have managed. what a race
The part from 4:16 to 4:36 shows just how much awareness Alonso has in a close fight.  First you see Ricciardo against Verstappen. Ricciardo defends on the inside. Verstappen takes a wider line into the corner, so that he can cross over to the inside on corner exit, carry more momentum out of the corner and attack on the next straight.   Then you see Alonso against Hamilton. The situation starts the exact same way, with Alonso on the inside. Hamilton takes a wider line, wants to carry more momentum, and against most other drivers this might have worked. But then Alonso lifts off the throttle in the middle of the corner! He slows down just enough so that Hamilton has to lift as well to avoid an accident. Hamilton's momentum is gone and Alonso accelerates away from him.  The spatial awareness from Alonso is incredible. If Hamilton were a little bit further back, this trick would not work, since HAM could just go around ALO. And if he were too close this would provoke an accident. But there is this tiny window where this trick works, and Alonso knows exactly when that is the case.  This is how he won that San Marino GP against Schumacher all these years back, and he has lost nothing of his racecraft since then.
